T 1613154851 18<20cmurf18>	that grubby became grubby-deprecated in fedora 30, the grubby we have now is a shell script for some tasks folks may be familiar with like setting default kernel to boot instead of using e.g. grub2-set-default or grub2-editenv directly
T 1613154879 18<20cmurf18>	the grub.cfg still contains os-prober entries like Windows and non-Fedora OS's

T 1613154990 18<20cmurf18>	you can still change command line options in /etc/default/grub, and run grub2-mkconfig (with or without -o, doesn't matter) and part of that script will modify just the options line in each bls snippet

T 1616529384 18<19dowdle18>	Yourmomuwu[m]: It also does updates what is considered the correct way these days... downloads everything and if needed will reboot the computer into an upgrade mode... do the upgrade and then give the graphical login back.  With dnf running inside of a GUI (unless under screen or tmux), there is always the risk of crashing something and messing up your package manager run.

T 1616611889 18<20cmurf18>	like you'd want to check swap in/out and compare it to page faults, once memory is reduced holding onto compressed anonymous pages it's possible that reclaim goes up i.e. any pages backed by a file like a library or config or binary can just be dropped to free up memory because it can be read back in from the file later
T 1616611907 18<20cmurf18>	so that reading it back in can look a lot like swap thrashing if it gets bad
T 1616611938 18<20cmurf18>	you see that in cases with too little or no swap or with a severly reduced swappiness value
T 1616611959 18<20cmurf18>	so yeah anyway it depends
